String(FloatMenu.innerHTML).replace(/font-size:11pt/gi, \'font-size:12pt\');                 FloatMenu.innerHTML = String(FloatMenu.innerHTML).replace(/font-size:10pt/gi, \'font-size:11pt\');             }             MenuMask.style.display = \'\';            FloatMenu.style.display = \'\';        } else {             MenuMask.style.display = \'none\';            FloatMenu.style.display = \'none\';        }     }     function SetTitleBar() {         setCookie(\'FLOAT_TITLE_BAR\',(getCookie(\'FLOAT_TITLE_BAR\')==\'T\'?\'F\':\'T\'),3650,\'/\');         imgSetTitleBar.src = \'image/pushpin\' +
